* Temporary quest followers are not marked.
NPCs marked with a skull and crossbones (<sup>☠</sup>) are dead.

[^a](#note_sithis) This person only appears after the completion of [Hail Sithis!](Skyrim_Hail_Sithis!.md). [^b](#note_madness) This person only appears if he survives [The Cure for Madness](Skyrim_The_Cure_for_Madness.md). [^c](#note_ferry) This [ferryman](Skyrim_Transport.md#Ferrymen DG) can be hired to transport you between cities via boat. [^d](#note_vigil) This person only appears during [Unholy Vigil](Skyrim_Unholy_Vigil.md). [^e](#note_thane) This person only appears after the completion of [Thane of the Pale](Skyrim_Thane_of_the_Pale.md). [^f](#note_rise) This person only appears during [Rise in the East](Skyrim_Rise_in_the_East.md).

| **[Argis the Bulwark](Skyrim_Argis_the_Bulwark.md)** [](Skyrim_Followers.md) | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |

[†](#note_Markarth Stall) These people only sell goods at the market. [‡](#note_Ghorza) Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure). [^a](#note_die To D) These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](Skyrim_The_Taste_of_Death.md) quest. [^b](#note_die FC) These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](Skyrim_The_Forsworn_Conspiracy.md) quest. [^c](#note_die NOECM) These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](Skyrim_No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine.md) quest. [^d](#note_die Enter) These people can die when you first enter the city. [^e](#note_die Ho H) Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](Skyrim_The_House_of_Horrors.md) quest. [^f](#note_Banning) Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance. [^g](#note_Fjotra) Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](Skyrim_The_Heart_of_Dibella.md).

[^c](#note_nohead) This person is executed upon first entering Solitude. [^d](#note_wedding) This person only appears during [Bound Until Death](Skyrim_Bound_Until_Death.md).

| **[Drovas Relvi](Skyrim_Drovas_Relvi.md)** †** <br> **[Varona Nelas](Skyrim_Varona_Nelas.md)** * | | | | | | | | | | |

† Found at the [Sun Stone](Skyrim_Sun_Stone.md) at night until the stone has been cleansed during the quest [Cleansing the Stones](Skyrim_Cleansing_the_Stones.md).
* Dies during the quest [Reluctant Steward](Skyrim_Reluctant_Steward.md).
** Appears after completing the quest [Reluctant Steward](Skyrim_Reluctant_Steward.md).

| **[Ysolda](Skyrim_Ysolda.md)** [](Skyrim_Inns.md) [](Skyrim_Merchants.md) †† | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | | |

* Only appears after [Dragon Rising](Skyrim_Dragon_Rising.md).
** Only appears after the [Stormcloaks](Skyrim_Stormcloaks.md) quest [Battle for Whiterun](Skyrim_Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks).md).
*** Only appears after the [Imperial Legion](Skyrim_Imperial_Legion.md) quest [Message to Whiterun](Skyrim_Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial).md).
**** Owns [Chillfurrow Farm](Skyrim_Chillfurrow_Farm.md) but sleeps here.
† This person only sells goods at the market.

†† Backup innkeeper for [Hulda](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda); also backup merchant for [Belethor](Skyrim_Belethor.md).

- ![PC Only](https://images.uesp.net/d/d7/Computer.svg)
The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Mod_Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

[^a](#note_market) Only sells goods at the market. [^b](#note_adelaisa) Only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](Skyrim_Dawnstar.md) with information during the relevant [quest](Skyrim_Rise_in_the_East.md) for Orthus. [^c](#note_brelasmalborn) Only present depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](Skyrim_Diplomatic_Immunity.md) quest. [^d](#note_ship) Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](Skyrim_Solstheim.md). [^e](#note_ferry) This [ferryman](Skyrim_Transport.md#Ferrymen DG) can be hired to transport you between cities via boat. [^f](#note_j.27datharr) Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](Skyrim_Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin.md).

| --- | --- |

These people are killed during [Alduin](Skyrim_Alduin.md)'s attack on Helgen. c. | [^](#note_Lokir) | |
| --- | --- |

[Lokir](Skyrim_Lokir.md) is killed during the opening cutscene while attempting to escape the Imperial Legion.

### [Thirsk People](Skyrim_Thirsk_Mead_Hall_People.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
Residents are only present at this location if you complete the quest [Retaking Thirsk](Skyrim_Retaking_Thirsk.md) in the Nords' favor. Before this point, they will be found at [Bujold's Retreat](Skyrim_Bujold%27s_Retreat.md) or elsewhere as noted.

**** Only while [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan) is active.
***** Only if the Imperials [regain control of the Rift](Skyrim_The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial).md).
‡ Only becomes innkeeper if Eydis is killed.

## Wanderers

### Caravans
| \| Ri'saad's Caravan \| <br> \| --- \| <br> \| **[Ri'saad](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad)** [](Skyrim_Merchants.md) <br> **[Khayla](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Khayla)**
